<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_379d7ee5-c8ec-4821-b2c7-256faec40672'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer2837482729997957565">Wrath volunteers to live and work outside Homeland, where he'll once again be confined in a small space with other males. He was subjected to horrific abuse and conditioning and forced to view endless sex tapes of human females while chained to Mercile's perverted machines. Wrath knows he's too dangerous and emotionally damaged to ever be with a female.<br/><br/>Lauren has just been</span>
  <span id="freeText2837482729997957565" style="display:none">Wrath volunteers to live and work outside Homeland, where he'll once again be confined in a small space with other males. He was subjected to horrific abuse and conditioning and forced to view endless sex tapes of human females while chained to Mercile's perverted machines. Wrath knows he's too dangerous and emotionally damaged to ever be with a female.<br /><br />Lauren has just been detained by three big, buff, well-armed men-New Species. One of them really catches her eye. He's tall, sexy and . . . her new roommate, apparently. Having never met a man this spectacular, she decides to taste every inch of his amazing body. Wrath is definitely open to that plan. The sex is incredible and he gives her everything she needs-but he'll only go so far. Something is holding him back.<br /><br />Lauren has to make him unleash his desire and Wrath has to get past his fear if the couple wants any chance at a future together.<br /><br />Publisher's Note: While each New Species book is a standalone, the greatest enjoyment will come from reading them in series order.</span>

Have some trust in yourself.”</b><br/><br/><br/>Wrath is the 6th book in the New Species Series, and it is a great read! Wrath has not tasted freedom for long. He still lives the nightmares of his sexual abuse and torture. Not feeling safe to be around females, and wanting to help others of his kind find freedom he joins the task force team. Him and a few of his team </span>

</a><br><br><b>“I know you won’t. You will be very gentle with me. I know that from the way you touch me. I trust you. Have some trust in yourself.”</b><br><br><br>Wrath is the 6th book in the New Species Series, and it is a great read! Wrath has not tasted freedom for long. He still lives the nightmares of his sexual abuse and torture. Not feeling safe to be around females, and wanting to help others of his kind find freedom he joins the task force team. Him and a few of his team mates are out trying to capture Bill, a ex Mercile employee. Instead a beautiful blonde shows up and it shocks him that he is attracted to her. Lauren makes him want things he feels he is too messed up to have. While holding her to find out what she knows about bill, she is attacked and he is made her protector, being around her all the time causes passions to ignite. Will he be able to get over his fears and past demons to have the woman he wants?<br><br><b>“Oh yeah,” Lauren gasped. “Doggy style is my favorite too.” Wrath lowered his head, kissed her neck and chuckled. “Canines do it best.”</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/BeFunky_81ab4ca5e7950c58971ca2b1472f0ede.jpg_zpset1pyvw1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

Even with all the demons from the past he never gives up. He is a fighter!<br><br><br><b>“I never believed I’d be attracted to a human female but you’re all I want.”<br><br><br>“I hope you meant it when you said I have you because I can’t let you go. You’re my mate, my other half, and my soul.”<br><br><br>“I can’t get enough of you. I have already scent imprinted you. I’m possessive and dominant. We keep being told that our kind has a deep-seated need to control the people around us but you control me. You look at me and I want to do anything to make you happy.”</b><br><br><br>Lauren made the book for me. She is very real and down to earth. She has a few extra pounds , but she is ok with that. She is beautiful inside and out. She was sassy, and a fighter. I love that she was so sweet and understanding of Wrath's past and the problems that he suffers from his abuse. She gives him love, support, and total trust. Letting him take things at his own pace, and willing to take whatever he feels he can give. I just loved her!!!<br><br><br><b>“I meant I don’t believe that you’d be rough with me and cause me pain. You’ve been nothing but wonderful. I admit my sexual experiences aren’t that vast but I wish you could see yourself the way I do now.”<br><br><br>“You’re amazing, strong, determined and brave. You hunt down those assholes that hurt your people. That’s so noble and yeah, brave. I admire you and think you’re the sexiest guy ever. I’m so glad you came into my life.”<br><br><br>“You make me happy. I hope I make you feel that way too. This…” She waved her hand at the room. “Doesn’t matter. It’s just being with you that does. I know your past and mine are drastically dissimilar but it’s the here and now that I care about.”</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/ce946e604c75826f670fe55068c0374a_zpsfyds8dnd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425063547i/13839331.jpg" alt=" photo ce946e604c75826f670fe55068c0374a_zpsfyds8dnd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>This book was a very enjoyable read, and added nicely to the continuing story line. Lauren and Wrath together are sweet, tender, but sexy too. I loved her best friend Amanda and I hope to see more of her... Maybe with Flame?? Wrath was a very nice addition to the series. I am on to the next book. Below I leave my favorite moment from the book.<br><br><br><b>“Ask me, Wrath. Please?” “I can’t. I’m not fit to be a mate and I have nothing to offer you.”That did it. Anger rose. “Nothing? You’re wonderful and amazing, Wrath. You’ve had such a rough life yet you’re the kindest man I’ve ever met. You’ve given me more in the short time we’ve had together than anyone else ever has. You risked your life to get me back. You fought for me when Vengeance went a little nuts and I love you. Do you know what it does to me when you hold me? I feel like I’m exactly where I belong. You touch me and I’ve never been so alive. You have scars inside and out but you faced your fears to make love to me. That’s the best gift anyone could give.” He shrugged off her hold. His hands rose to cup her cheeks and leaned down until their faces were just a few mere inches apart and searched her eyes. She wasn’t sure what he looked for but she knew he’d find honestly. “I won’t ever let you go if you agree to be my mate. Ever. It won’t be easy but I’d do anything for you to make you happy. I would die if you ever left me. I couldn’t survive missing you.” “I choose you, Wrath. Always you. You’re not going to lose me.”</b><br><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jessicasoverthetopbookobsession.blogspot.com/">http://jessicasoverthetopbookobsessio...</a></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1623376304" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17134639212198289023"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>She’s mine. She said she feels love for me. Take her. Keep her. Mine!</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>This is the sixth installment in New Species series and it was way better than I had originally expected. I admit I’ve found this series is kind of hit and miss. Mostly miss. So it was a huge surprise for me that I enjoyed every page of this book, and the characters as well, were all likable.<br/><br/>Even though the plot was a bit simple and predictable, the author delivered this fun and entertaining read in which I had a ha</span>
  <span id="freeText17134639212198289023" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>She’s mine. She said she feels love for me. Take her. Keep her. Mine!</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />This is the sixth installment in New Species series and it was way better than I had originally expected. I admit I’ve found this series is kind of hit and miss. Mostly miss. So it was a huge surprise for me that I enjoyed every page of this book, and the characters as well, were all likable.<br /><br />Even though the plot was a bit simple and predictable, the author delivered this fun and entertaining read in which I had a hard time putting it down.<br /><br />Wrath is an endearing New Species. I loved everything about him. I loved his strong physical body as much as his honesty, protectiveness, possessiveness, determination, and selflessness towards Lauren. But most of all, the thing that made my heart melt was the way he treated her with such tenderness and sweetness. When a very big guy did something like that, I just couldn’t say no.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Always, Lauren,” he whispered. “I give you my life, my loyalty and my heart forever.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />Lauren is a smart and strong woman. She could handle difficult situations bravely and cleverly. She’s somewhat different from other Laurann Dohner’s heroines, and I liked that very much.<br /><br />The flammable sexual tension between Wrath and Lauren was manifest from the beginning. The sex was scorching hot that you should keep a very big fan near you. I found myself smiling involuntarily throughout those scenes where they spent time together. They were really meant for each other.<br /><br />As much as I enjoyed reading this book, the only thing that kept me from rating it 5 stars was the filler. There were too many scenes that felt like needless fillers and some parts of the story dragged a bit. But on the whole it was good and appealing.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I will learn to be the best mate.”<br />He was so damn cute and if he didn’t already have her heart, he would have won it over in that moment. She reached up and traced his cheekbone. “You already are the best.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />By the way, I’m happy I picked up this book. I was so satisfied with ‘MINE’—got what I wanted already!<br /><br /><br />---------------------------------<br /><br /><br />**BR with my fellow NS lovers, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/4150124-aileene" rel="nofollow noopener">Aileene</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/27279812-future-jess-the-book-eating-dinosaur-nynaeve" rel="nofollow noopener">Jess</a>.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1599062968" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4978201092419896050"><b>Sorry, what was that?</b><br/><br/>I couldn't hear you over the sound of my internal screaming about the way rape was used as a plot device in this.<br/><br/>Sure, New Species books <u>ALWAYS</u> have the token rape attempt, the hero swoops in and then YAY it's back to happy fun sexy times. <br/><br/>But this book? <b>This book took that idea and fucking flew it to the moon</b>. <br/><br/>If Lauren wasn't being accosted by Vengeance, she was being scared into compliance by Wrath with the threat of Vengeance coming after her again. And then when she is </span>
  <span id="freeText4978201092419896050" style="display:none"><b>Sorry, what was that?</b><br /><br />I couldn't hear you over the sound of my internal screaming about the way rape was used as a plot device in this.<br /><br />Sure, New Species books <u>ALWAYS</u> have the token rape attempt, the hero swoops in and then YAY it's back to happy fun sexy times. <br /><br />But this book? <b>This book took that idea and fucking flew it to the moon</b>. <br /><br />If Lauren wasn't being accosted by Vengeance, she was being scared into compliance by Wrath with the threat of Vengeance coming after her again. And then when she is back in the real world she is kidnapped <i>AGAIN</i> and threatened with sexual violence numerous times from both human and New Species men. <br /><br />She was threatened with sexual assault so many times I found it hard to actually pay attention to the rest of the story, because the pattern that was established early on here was that no matter what Lauren did, she was going to be threatened in some capacity. <br /><br />I didn't really buy the love story here. But it was refreshing to have characters that actually talked to each other, didn't create problems for each other with silly issues of miscommunication and there was no token asshole character getting in the middle of their relationship.<br /><br />On the whole this was a big miss for me. <br /><br />But I'm a sucker so of course I will keep reading this series. Because mind-crack and all that.<br /><br /><b>2</b> <i>lets-go-jack-off-in-the-shower</i> <b>Stars</b><br /><br />Thanks for the buddy read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1470105427" rel="nofollow noopener">Aileene</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/26653561-alp" rel="nofollow noopener">Alp</a>!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer280168830" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15268185196910222978">First off let me say, I have really enjoyed this series thus far and so I was eagerly anticipating the release of Wrath (who wouldn't with a cover hottie like that). It's the same formula that the other books in the series has relied on. New Species meets girl. Girl meets New Species. New Species likes girl. Girl likes New Species. Sex ensues. Then the girl gets kidnapped. New Species gets mad and saves her. More sex. Then love. Then we get our happily ever after. <br/><br/>I may sound flippant (it's my w</span>
  <span id="freeText15268185196910222978" style="display:none">First off let me say, I have really enjoyed this series thus far and so I was eagerly anticipating the release of Wrath (who wouldn't with a cover hottie like that). It's the same formula that the other books in the series has relied on. New Species meets girl. Girl meets New Species. New Species likes girl. Girl likes New Species. Sex ensues. Then the girl gets kidnapped. New Species gets mad and saves her. More sex. Then love. Then we get our happily ever after. <br /><br />I may sound flippant (it's my way) but like I said, I really have enjoyed the series and the premise of these books thus far. But Wrath, Wrath just fell flat for me. I couldn't connect with the characters, the dialogue felt stilted, especially between the H&amp;h, and cheesy. I also couldn't get when or how the H&amp;h fell in love and the whole <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Vengeance tries to rape Lauren, not once but twice, and she appears over it in a few hours (later in the book she says to Wrath "You fought for me when Vengeance went a little nuts and I love you"... a LITTLE nuts...really!!) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I really wish I had liked this book more! I've loved all of the other NS books so perhaps my expectations were a little to high. I'll still read the next in the series and just hope this is a one off aberration. <br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer18299757780348554546"><b>Re-read Dec 16-18, 2016</b><br/><br/>I really enjoyed this instalment of New Species, I remember 919 from the last book <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13107655.Brawn__New_Species___5_' title='Brawn (New Species, #5) by Laurann Dohner' rel='nofollow noopener'>Brawn</a> and felt so bad for him.   <span id="freeText18299757780348554546" style="display:none"><b>Re-read Dec 16-18, 2016</b><br /><br />I really enjoyed this instalment of New Species, I remember 919 from the last book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13107655.Brawn__New_Species___5_" title="Brawn (New Species, #5) by Laurann Dohner" rel="nofollow noopener">Brawn</a> and felt so bad for him. I disagree with all the reviewers that said the writing was choppy and the dialogue not realistic. You have to take into account that Wrath is newly freed and has not been exposed to human language all that much. <br /><br />I found it very steamy overall and kinda endearing that Wrath was so cautious and hesitant at first. He just wants to protect Lauren and make sure he doesn't hurt her if he gets a flashback of his abuse. Thankfully Shadow is there to back him up and lend support. They have a deep bond since they've been through so much together.<br /><br />I got to see my favorite guy Brass...still hoping he gets a book (hint hint). I did find Amanda a bit annoying (and hilarious) but I'm curious to find out if she hooks up with Flame (another hottie). Lauren was so smart and brave and she never gave up on Wrath. He's so cute when he says that he will learn to be the best mate ever. <br /></span>

<div id="review_269965854" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/269965854" />
    <a title="Jess the Romanceaholic" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2807469-jess-the-romanceaholic"><img alt="Jess the Romanceaholic" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1298615023p2/2807469.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/269965854?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jess the Romanceaholic" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jess the Romanceaholic" href="/user/show/2807469-jess-the-romanceaholic">Jess the Romanceaholic</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2807469-jess-the-romanceaholic?shelf=raped-or-abused">raped-or-abused</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2807469-jess-the-romanceaholic?shelf=realistically-sized-heroine">realistically-sized-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2807469-jess-the-romanceaholic?shelf=steam-level-steamy">steam-level-steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2807469-jess-the-romanceaholic?shelf=on-the-run">on-the-run</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2807469-jess-the-romanceaholic?shelf=2012-read">2012-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2807469-jess-the-romanceaholic?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2807469-jess-the-romanceaholic?shelf=kidnapped">kidnapped</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer269965854" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7610709678325257957">I should probably establish a few things before I really get into the meat of the review here.<br/><br/>First, I'm a big fan of this series. I freely acknowledge that this series is a Guilty Pleasure of mine, because frankly, the writing is pretty bad. Incredibly stilted dialog, ridiculous situations, and of course horrific abuse from caricature villains.<br/><br/>Normally, I enjoy it anyway. <br/><br/>This book, however, was an enormous let-down. I'm not quite sure if it's simply the fact that I've read the entire series an</span>
  <span id="freeText7610709678325257957" style="display:none">I should probably establish a few things before I really get into the meat of the review here.<br /><br />First, I'm a big fan of this series. I freely acknowledge that this series is a Guilty Pleasure of mine, because frankly, the writing is pretty bad. Incredibly stilted dialog, ridiculous situations, and of course horrific abuse from caricature villains.<br /><br />Normally, I enjoy it anyway. <br /><br />This book, however, was an enormous let-down. I'm not quite sure if it's simply the fact that I've read the entire series and so "the formula" is getting really old for me, or if it's simply that this book jumped the shark for me. <br /><br />I was excited to learn that the heroine is a little plump ("needs to lose 30 lbs"), and of course love seeing a traumatized New Species male get past his history and find love. <br /><br />I even enjoyed the premise behind how Wrath and Lauren ended up spending time together. <br /><br />However. <br /><br />The dialog is stilted. True, it's <i>always</i> stilted, and Ms. Dohner has <i>always</i> been notorious for telling instead of showing in every book of hers that I've read, but it seemed quite a bit more pronounced in this one.<br /><br />Wrath's supposed hatred of human females fell <i>horribly</i> flat, and Lauren's reactions to some of the events in the story were really unrealistic.<br /><br />Add into that Lauren's friend Amanda and her over-the-top behavior, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[yet <i>another</i> Mercile kidnapping <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, and some very tame love scenes, and I was just flat out sorry I'd spent my money on this one. <br /><br />2/5 Stars, and I can only hope that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13107666.Tiger__New_Species___7_" title="Tiger (New Species, #7) by Laurann Dohner" rel="nofollow noopener">Tiger</a> will be better, or I might truly be done with this series. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7610709678325257957" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer12295485868622091522">5++ Stars!!<br/><br/>Yep!! <span id="freeTextContainer17952488257620768324">What a nice addition to the <i>New Species</i> series!!! :)<br/><br/>I loved <b>Wrath</b> and his 'chubby', smart, little <b>Lauren</b>!<br/><br/>I think that's the best book of the series so far, and I liked both of the MCs. In some previous books either the NSO male or the human female sometimes got on my nerves and I was surprised with some pairings... ;)<br/><br/>IMHO, <b>Lauren</b> is the best NS series heroine since <b>Doc Trisha</b> in Book 2. She's not a slim beauty, she's a bit chubby, but she's also very clever and quick-witted, which saves her in m</span>
  <span id="freeText17952488257620768324" style="display:none">What a nice addition to the <i>New Species</i> series!!! :)<br /><br />I loved <b>Wrath</b> and his 'chubby', smart, little <b>Lauren</b>!<br /><br />I think that's the best book of the series so far, and I liked both of the MCs. In some previous books either the NSO male or the human female sometimes got on my nerves and I was surprised with some pairings... ;)<br /><br />IMHO, <b>Lauren</b> is the best NS series heroine since <b>Doc Trisha</b> in Book 2. She's not a slim beauty, she's a bit chubby, but she's also very clever and quick-witted, which saves her in many situations. She doesn't have to be a 'badass' heroine, like <b>Jessie</b> in Book 4 to be able to rescue his beloved from kidnappers - awkwardly and with some help like a 'normal' human being and not some superhero ;) - and also to save herself and 5 other New Species from the sick f*cks who were holding them. <br /><br /><b>Wrath</b>, on the other hand, is the sweetest NS male in the whole series (I've read 6 first books so far) :) He's newly freed, still so unsure of himself and the world outside of the cage, yet he instantly feels what's good and what's bad. He's cute and so caring about Lauren and her well-being, even after the tremendous abuse (also sexual) he had suffered from Mercile Industries. He's strong enough to face and combat his fears and very thoughful towards new things, sensations and concepts. He simply stole my heart! ;)<br /><br />I'm skipping 2 books now as I'm very curious of <b>Shadow</b>'s story! He's Wrath's best friend, a brother by choice, and he also seems very different from other NSO males. He's intriguing :)<br /><br />I'm so looking forward to <b>Tiger</b>'s book - he's such a 'confirmed bachelor' in NS terms, never wanting anything to do with females and finding a mate. I'm very curious of a girl who finally ensnares him! ;) For now I need something 'sweeter', though... Hence, I'm starting Shadow's book now, especially keenly since the other MC is <b>Beauty </b>, a 'Gift Female' (finally!) and I'd really love to see her get some love and happiness ;) </span>
  <a data-text-id="17952488257620768324" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9558554741448441338">I was hesitant to read this one because quite a few people had rated this low and I guess it just proved that I shouldn't feel influenced by others people's opinion, because I really enjoyed this.<br/><br/>I loved that the heroine was heavier and not stick thin. I loved that both the hero and heroine battled with their own insecurities and I love it because it shows me a vulnerable side of their characters and appeals to me emotionally. <br/><br/>The heroine and her best friend, Amanda, we're hilarious together. I </span>
  <span id="freeText9558554741448441338" style="display:none">I was hesitant to read this one because quite a few people had rated this low and I guess it just proved that I shouldn't feel influenced by others people's opinion, because I really enjoyed this.<br /><br />I loved that the heroine was heavier and not stick thin. I loved that both the hero and heroine battled with their own insecurities and I love it because it shows me a vulnerable side of their characters and appeals to me emotionally. <br /><br />The heroine and her best friend, Amanda, we're hilarious together. I desperately hope something does happen between Flame and Amanda. Flame deserves his own mate and Amanda is more than infatuated with him. I wonder if they will get their own book. I sure hope so. <br /><br />Wrath was adorable and I wasn't expecting that. Every time he voiced or thought that he so badly wanted to be the best mate for Lauren and you could just see how badly he wanted it and how much he was trying... It was so sweet, heartwarming and completely swoon worthy. <br /><br />I know the plot is formulaic and I'm really hoping that the next few books will have something different. And even though some of it was recycled material, I still enjoyed it.<br /><br />Tiger has played quite large roles in some of the previous books so I'm very curious to see who he will be mated with and what their relationship will be like. I'm looking forward to driving into his book and getting to know him even better.</span>

    <a title="Noura " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17896144-noura"><img alt="Noura " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1476924036p2/17896144.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1698501907?book_show_action=true">Jul 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Noura " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Noura " href="/user/show/17896144-noura">Noura </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1698501907" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4928757360905198810">Before i start....i just want to say that bookcover is awesome.<br/><br/>Ok.....this one's quite interesting - we have Brawn, a newly freed New Species who's joined the human task force (the one that rescues New Species that are still in captivity) falling for a human female that was mistakenly thought to be part of the Mercile staff still at lose.<br/><br/>Of course there's the expected instant-attraction between them but Brawn is reluctant in pursuing Lauren because she's human a.k.a very fragile beings therefore</span>
  <span id="freeText4928757360905198810" style="display:none">Before i start....i just want to say that bookcover is awesome.<br><br>Ok.....this one's quite interesting - we have Brawn, a newly freed New Species who's joined the human task force (the one that rescues New Species that are still in captivity) falling for a human female that was mistakenly thought to be part of the Mercile staff still at lose.<br><br>Of course there's the expected instant-attraction between them but Brawn is reluctant in pursuing Lauren because she's human a.k.a very fragile beings therefore will not be able to endure the rough and intense passion of NS style shagging (duhhh....really....after awhile this gets kind of old). There were parts of the story where Lauren was shamed because she's "over-weight" therefore "desperate" for someone to want her (a real and common misconception among people who are image-prejudiced). I really like the lead gal in this one because she's really smart and funny. But i really like her best friend Amanda because she's just hilarious! I wonder if she's going to have her own HEA with a NS guy. <br><br>All in all, this one's quite an adventurous ride. There're multiple kidnappings, suspense, sweet moments, really funny dialogues (between Lauren and Amanda mostly) and lots of super-sexy moments (especially the shower scene. Brawn. YASSSSSS!!!!)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469166236i/19787220._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ooops...heads up: there are also two scenes of attempted sexual assault, so be warned. <br><br>A fun read. I'm on to my next one. <br></span>

<div id="review_289783431" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/289783431" />
    <a title="Heather" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3841282-heather"><img alt="Heather" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1538524996p2/3841282.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/289783431?book_show_action=true">Mar 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather" href="/user/show/3841282-heather">Heather</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3841282-heather?shelf=scifi">scifi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3841282-heather?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3841282-heather?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3841282-heather?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3841282-heather?shelf=mediocre">mediocre</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3841282-heather?shelf=non-con">non-con</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3841282-heather?shelf=abusive-control-freak-characters">abusive-control-freak-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3841282-heather?shelf=boring">boring</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3841282-heather?shelf=bad-writing">bad-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3841282-heather?shelf=laurann-dohner">laurann-dohner</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer289783431" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4976412417490635522">Fresh off of a streak of Lora Leigh, and the seriously dark and twisted R.Lee Smith, I realized it had been a while since I could really let my brain go with a book. I needed some lighter fare that would be easier on my psyche. Lucky for me, Wrath had just been released, and I quickly downloaded it to my kindle. And I have to say, it delivered, in every way I expected it to:<br/><br/>*Bad dialogue, awkwardly written conversations, like this little gem:<br/><i>"I like the name Shadow. I like to stand still and wat</i></span>
  <span id="freeText4976412417490635522" style="display:none">Fresh off of a streak of Lora Leigh, and the seriously dark and twisted R.Lee Smith, I realized it had been a while since I could really let my brain go with a book. I needed some lighter fare that would be easier on my psyche. Lucky for me, Wrath had just been released, and I quickly downloaded it to my kindle. And I have to say, it delivered, in every way I expected it to:<br /><br />*Bad dialogue, awkwardly written conversations, like this little gem:<br /><i>"I like the name Shadow. I like to stand still and watch others."</i><br />and<br /><i>"You will be my mate and do as I ask by taking me to Bill. You no longer belong to him and will carry my scent."</i><br />*A gruff, possessive alpha hero with issues<br />*A kind-hearted, boring-as-hell "everyday career woman" heroine<br />*The hero's likeable best friend who will surely be getting a book of his own<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[*Attempted rape used as a plot device...twice, in fact. <br />*The exact same plotline as in every single New Species story: Heroine is thrown together with Hero, vanilla sex happens, they face his dark personality/emotional issues together. Heroine is kidnapped by Mercile, then rescued by Hero. HEA!<br /><br />In this case, our heroine is Lauren Henderson, a plucky and plump little real estate agent unknowingly working for some ex-Mercile thugs. A typically shallow girl's lunch between Lauren her BFF Amanda reveals to us some very compelling information that is pertinent to the story: that both women are blonde, Lauren is short, has big boobs, is blue-eyed, and 30 lbs overweight; and Amanda is not short, doesn't have blue eyes or big boobs, and is 60 lbs overweight. And both women have histories of heartbreak in the romance department. <br /><br />Of our hero? Well he's introduced as "919", a male we met in Brawn, who in a fit of madness, attacked Becca who then was defended by Brawn. Apparentally 919 is a bit calmer these days, and in a name choosing ceremony-of-sorts, he chooses the name Wrath. In the labs, Wrath was force-masturbated by a machine while watching pornographic images of human women. Consequently, he supposedly has lots of rage toward human women and is afraid to engage in sex, believing he couldn't keep control. All of that changes of course, when he meets Lauren. She tempts him the way no other woman has, not that he's had a lot of opportunity to meet other women. After kidnapping her and then saving her from not one, but TWO attempted rapes by the same guy, a fellow new species named Vengeance, the two can't resist the supposed heat that we're informed exists between them. And inspite of having her clothes torn off twice in one evening, and being sexually assaulted to an extent, Lauren can't help but feel horny. I mean, who could blame her right? Just look at that book cover! And her reasoning? A girl like herself could never do better than a guy that looks like Wrath. Wrath's sexual issues ended up being so overblown. The erotic scenes were a let-down, and certain canine "swelling" aspects of his anatomy were a little too reminiscent of other series I've read. There was no real loss of control, no rage, no pain during sex. It was so boring I skimmed.<br /><br />We're given an obligatory scene where Amanda meets Wrath and drools over him, and blatantly comes on to him sexually, at Lauren's work no less. This scene was so unbelievable I almost stopped reading the book right then. Amanda came across as a desperate and pathetic slut. If Dohner was trying to establish her as a sexually bold modern woman, she could have done so in a much less cheesey and awkward way, and had Amanda maintain some of her dignity. After helping Lauren save Wrath from the ex-Mercile guys, she then meets Flame, and it's heavily foreshadowed that they will be a couple. <br /><br />Through the kidnapping, we meet new New Species, including 140, a feline New Species whose mate was being held hostage until the big rescue at the end. His mate interestingly enough, is supposed to be a primate type, which I found a little odd. It seems that Laurann Dohner is breaking with tradition in having interspecies matings. It doesn't really make a lot of sense though. And I wonder if they would reproduce? 140 keeps Lauren warm while they are locked up together, which predictably leads to Wrath freaking out over Lauren having another male's scent on her. He scubs the crap out of her body head to toe and immediately scent marks her, since she's pretty much his property, and isn't allowed to even touch other men. It's super romantic and loving. And conveniently enough, Lauren has no real life, since her job no longer exists and her family lives across the country. She has no hobbies or outside interests, and only one friend, so she has no problem giving up everything to be Wrath's woman. They get married at the end. Yay!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />All in all, these books are starting to become more of a chore to read, I've decided. I think I still read them because I've read every one in the series so far, so it feels sort of like an obligation now. The storyline is not moving along at all, and each new book plays exactly the same. The dialogue is childish, overly simplistic, and awkward. It stood out a lot in this book, and frankly, makes the New Species look mentally deficient. They all sound child-like and cavemanish when they speak. They have simple minds and simple personalities. I almost find it kind of insulting to men, to be honest. I'll probably read Tiger, but if that too sucks, I'm declaring myself over this series. <br /> <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4976412417490635522" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Edwina &quot; I LoveBooks&quot; &quot;Deb&quot;" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Edwina &quot; I LoveBooks&quot; &quot;Deb&quot;" href="/user/show/6255709-edwina-i-lovebooks-deb">Edwina &quot; I LoveBooks&quot; &quot;Deb&quot;</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer367014756" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14496446201293402385">WOW!! This a another fasted pace, hard to put down New Species story. Wrath was feature as 919 who we met in Brawn's book, he had been really abuse in the Mercile facility. He is constantly forced to spill his sperm by this weird sex machine to be sold in Europe for breeding purposes. Wrath has been rescued and is now working on the NSO Task Force. The Task Force accidentally kidnaps Lauren while setting a trap for and Ex Mercile Technician, Brent, believing she is in alliance with Mercile Indus</span>
  <span id="freeText14496446201293402385" style="display:none">WOW!! This a another fasted pace, hard to put down New Species story. Wrath was feature as 919 who we met in Brawn's book, he had been really abuse in the Mercile facility. He is constantly forced to spill his sperm by this weird sex machine to be sold in Europe for breeding purposes. Wrath has been rescued and is now working on the NSO Task Force. The Task Force accidentally kidnaps Lauren while setting a trap for and Ex Mercile Technician, Brent, believing she is in alliance with Mercile Industries they take her to their headquarters for questioning.<br /><br />Let me just say both Wrath and Lauren are very easy characters to fall in love with. We watch Wrath trying to over come his abuse and Lauren trying to overcome the fact that she is overweight. They are both very wounded individuals, but together they make one of the strongest couples in the series. Lauren is very intelligent and thinks on her feet to get herself and Wrath out of being captured by Mercil. Lauren has a friend name Amanda who is also, overweight and looking for love.<br /><br /> You are going to love Amanda and I hope she gets a story or at least we get to revisit her again. I would love to have a girlfriend like Amanda.<br /><br />Their are some sad moments in the story, but their are some LOL moments with Lauren and Amanda and Amanda and the New Species she comes in contact with. Don't let me forget, the Love Making Scenes are Hot and off the Chart SIZZLING!! We also, get to meet a lot of new; New Species, being introduced in the story and we revisit some of our old friend. This is a must read and I highly recommend this series to everyone!!<br /><br />I can't wait for April 10th Tiger's book comes out YEAH TIGER!!!<br /><br />Re Read 2/19/18 </span>

  <span id="freeText1346858738833635518" style="display:none">Wrath has made great strides since he arrived at Homeland, but he still longs for a little solitude and time to adjust. Wrath decides to volunteer to be part of a small unit working outside of Homeland, figuring this will give him the space he needs. When the team grabs Lauren, believing has ties to Mercile corp, Wrath finds himself unbelievable attracted to her and forced to protect her.<br /><br />Wrath's time at Mercile has left him believing he wont be able to control himself when it comes to human women. On every level he wants Lauren, but he is unwilling to put her in danger and continues to keep her at a distance. Lauren is determined to prove to Wrath that he is in control of everything he does, pushing him to unknown boundaries and hoping that what they are experiencing is not only for a short time.<br /><br /><br />Full review on Sensual Reads<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://sensualreads.com/?p=9401">http://sensualreads.com/?p=9401</a></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('830uVcDowif2mhAHk32wXn2g5wRjB6V+ia/BU2VRZzbEHXWPiYDH+EgFV0DYVmRm/J8T7vJlfUUkeKXLyXdDBw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Tq7JZgA0L3CmytpcjcroTFRw6Jg/08hSAykZm+PJoyN5zpK8SVwqrxhVnRvG4Tx01U8ccq6xEGmu/n0DT++HEg==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer2632290322898992821">I had a rather short area here telling a little about me but then I had more than a few people ask me to expand it so... here goes. LOL. I'm a full time home 'supervisor' which is a nice word for saying I'm a housewife. I'm married happily, I met my dream guy 20 years ago, and we have 4 children. I live in Southern California and I can't function without iced coffee. I believe in romance, I've alw</span>
  <span id="freeText2632290322898992821" style="display:none">I had a rather short area here telling a little about me but then I had more than a few people ask me to expand it so... here goes. LOL. I'm a full time home 'supervisor' which is a nice word for saying I'm a housewife. I'm married happily, I met my dream guy 20 years ago, and we have 4 children. I live in Southern California and I can't function without iced coffee. I believe in romance, I've always been a daydreamer, and I'm a HUGE fan of books, always have been.<br /><br />No, I didn't know that I always wanted to write. I inhaled books as a child. I read entire series (Pippi Longstocking, Nancy Drew and The Hardy Boys, Trixie Beldon, The Borrowers, etc) in a matter of days at a time. By the time I was nine years old I had an adult library card where I visited often. I moved on to John Saul, Stephen King, Richard Laymon, Agatha Christie, and then found romance. I was hooked. I wrote poetry in my teens and then moved on to short stories. My first book was started after I read a real bomb of a book that ticked me off with really horrible characters and a plot that was shabby at best and I thought... I could do better. LOL.<br /><br />I wrote my first book which will probably never see the light of day in the early 90's. I wrote a series of a few books from it. I'm a series fan! I kept writing for fun, wrote MANY books and then in 2009 I decided to try to get published. I wrote my first Sci Fi romance and Ral's Woman came to be. I submitted it and with a little tweaking, Ellorascave sent me an acceptance letter. It was kind of a 'Cinderella' experience for me. It's been a terrific ride so far and I'm really happy that I finally had the time to commit to writing full time. It's a dream come true.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2632290322898992821" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        });
      $('bookCover_17987085').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
